RRGM Dictionary v1.0
Section: T-Z
License: CC BY-SA 4.0
Scope: Core English + RRGM bridge semantic operating layer.
Provenance: Source-preservation split from project dictionary files, with recovered entries inserted and ES cleanup only.
Note: Do not treat every entry as legal, medical, technical, or clinical authority. This is a semantic bridge/corpus layer.

Entry count: 1780
Letters included: T, U, V, W, X, Y, Z

===== T =====

T001 table
Common meaning:
A piece of furniture with a flat top, or an organized set of information in rows and columns.
Example:
The book was on the table.
RRGM bridge:
Table is support or arrangement ES. It can hold objects physically or organize information for recognition.

T002 take
Common meaning:
To get, hold, carry, remove, accept, or choose.
Example:
She took the key from the drawer.
RRGM bridge:
Take moves something into possession, access, or action. It must be checked for permission when another boundary is involved.

T003 talk
Common meaning:
To speak with someone or communicate by words.
Example:
They talked after dinner.
RRGM bridge:
Talk is relation-signal exchange. It can carry meaning, care, pressure, repair, or conflict.

T004 tall
Common meaning:
Greater than average height.
Example:
The tall tree shaded the yard.
RRGM bridge:
Tall marks vertical scale. It should be read relative to a reference field.

T005 target
Common meaning:
A goal, object, person, place, or point aimed at.
Example:
The arrow hit the target.
RRGM bridge:
Target is selected focus. It directs action, attention, risk, or measurement toward a specific point.

T006 task
Common meaning:
A job, duty, or piece of work to be done.
Example:
The task was to sort the files.
RRGM bridge:
Task is bounded work-path. It defines purpose, expected output, and completion gate.

T007 teach
Common meaning:
To help someone learn knowledge, skill, or understanding.
Example:
She taught the child to read.
RRGM bridge:
Teach creates learning support. It transfers pattern through guidance, practice, correction, and care.

T008 team
Common meaning:
A group working together toward a goal.
Example:
The team finished the project.
RRGM bridge:
Team is coordinated relation ES. It distributes task, trust, support, responsibility, and risk.

T009 tear
Common meaning:
A drop from the eye, or a rip in material depending on pronunciation and context.
Example:
A tear rolled down her cheek.
RRGM bridge:
Tear must be context-bound. It can mark grief signal or structural break.

T010 tell
Common meaning:
To communicate, explain, report, or identify.
Example:
She told him the truth.
RRGM bridge:
Tell moves meaning into another recognition field. It can support truth, pressure, repair, or harm.

T011 term
Common meaning:
A word, phrase, condition, period, or agreed rule.
Example:
The term was defined in the glossary.
RRGM bridge:
Term is named meaning unit or condition. It needs domain and context to avoid drift.

T012 test
Common meaning:
A method used to check knowledge, quality, function, or truth.
Example:
The test showed the battery was weak.
RRGM bridge:
Test is recognition gate. It must fit the domain, claim, and stakes.

T013 text
Common meaning:
Written or typed words.
Example:
The text explained the process.
RRGM bridge:
Text is language ES. It carries meaning through symbols, sequence, context, and reader recognition.

T014 than
Common meaning:
A word used for comparison.
Example:
This box is heavier than that one.
RRGM bridge:
Than creates comparison relation. It requires a reference scale and compared property.

T015 thank
Common meaning:
To express gratitude.
Example:
She thanked him for the help.
RRGM bridge:
Thank signals recognition of support, care, or value. Gratitude should not erase boundary or debt-pressure.

T016 that
Common meaning:
A word used to point to, identify, connect, or introduce a clause.
Example:
That book is mine.
RRGM bridge:
That is reference language. It links attention to a specific pattern, claim, or relation.

T017 the
Common meaning:
A word used to mark a specific person, thing, group, or idea.
Example:
The door was open.
RRGM bridge:
The narrows reference. It tells the receiver that a specific pattern is being indicated.

T018 their
Common meaning:
Belonging to or associated with them.
Example:
Their house was near the river.
RRGM bridge:
Their marks relation, possession, or association. It should preserve group and individual boundary where relevant.

T019 them
Common meaning:
A pronoun referring to people, animals, things, or ideas already mentioned.
Example:
I gave them the notes.
RRGM bridge:
Them carries reference across sequence. It preserves continuity of a previously named pattern.

T020 then
Common meaning:
At that time, next, or as a result.
Example:
She read the note, then smiled.
RRGM bridge:
Then marks sequence or consequence. It connects one state to another through time or logic.

T021 theory
Common meaning:
An explanation or system of ideas used to understand something.
Example:
The theory explained the pattern.
RRGM bridge:
Theory is structured meaning model. It organizes claims, evidence, predictions, and reality gates.

T022 there
Common meaning:
In or at that place, or used to show existence.
Example:
The keys are there.
RRGM bridge:
There marks location or existence in a field. It anchors attention away from the speaker’s immediate position.

T023 these
Common meaning:
Plural of this; used to point to nearby or specific things.
Example:
These files are important.
RRGM bridge:
These marks selected nearby patterns. It narrows the recognition field to a specific group.

T024 they
Common meaning:
A pronoun referring to people, beings, things, or groups already mentioned.
Example:
They arrived early.
RRGM bridge:
They carries group or singular reference through sequence. It preserves pattern continuity without repeating the name.

T025 thing
Common meaning:
An object, idea, event, action, or unspecified item.
Example:
That thing on the shelf is broken.
RRGM bridge:
Thing is broad placeholder language. It should be replaced with a specific noun when precision matters.

T026 think
Common meaning:
To use the mind, consider, believe, reason, or form an idea.
Example:
She thought about the answer.
RRGM bridge:
Think is cognition-process language. In DI, it should be mapped by domain as processing, reasoning, selection, or model-state change.

T027 this
Common meaning:
A word used to point to something nearby, current, or specific.
Example:
This page has the answer.
RRGM bridge:
This anchors attention to the active field. It marks the current pattern, claim, or object.

T028 thought
Common meaning:
An idea, belief, act of thinking, or mental content.
Example:
The thought stayed with her.
RRGM bridge:
Thought is cognition content or process trace. In DI, it should be domain-bound, not forced into human-only meaning.

T029 thread
Common meaning:
A thin strand, a line of discussion, or connected sequence.
Example:
The thread connected the comments.
RRGM bridge:
Thread is continuity path. It links parts across sequence so meaning can be followed.

T030 through
Common meaning:
Moving in one side and out another, by means of, or continuing across.
Example:
The light passed through the window.
RRGM bridge:
Through names passage path or courier. It shows how a pattern crosses support, medium, or relation.

T031 time
Common meaning:
The measure or experience of sequence, duration, or when something happens.
Example:
The time was midnight.
RRGM bridge:
Time marks sequence and change. In RRGM-adjacent use, time should often be read through decay, transition, and state-change.

T032 tiny
Common meaning:
Very small.
Example:
The tiny seed grew into a tree.
RRGM bridge:
Tiny marks very low scale. Tiny does not mean unimportant; small structures can be load-bearing.

T033 title
Common meaning:
A name given to a book, work, role, position, or section.
Example:
The title of the paper was clear.
RRGM bridge:
Title is recognition handle. It frames expectation, role, authority, or meaning.

T034 to
Common meaning:
A word showing direction, relation, purpose, recipient, or infinitive verb form.
Example:
She went to the store.
RRGM bridge:
To creates direction or relation path. It points movement, intention, or transfer toward a target.

T035 together
Common meaning:
With each other, in one place, or combined.
Example:
They worked together.
RRGM bridge:
Together marks coupling or shared field. It can support emergence, care, pressure, or capture depending on boundary.

T036 token
Common meaning:
A symbol, unit, sign, small piece, or digital language unit.
Example:
The system counted each token.
RRGM bridge:
Token is small counted signal unit. It can carry partial meaning, but not total meaning alone.

T037 tone
Common meaning:
The quality, feeling, or attitude in sound, speech, writing, or color.
Example:
Her tone was gentle.
RRGM bridge:
Tone shapes signal meaning. It carries pressure, care, irony, refusal, or dignity beyond words alone.

T038 tool
Common meaning:
An object, method, or system used to do work.
Example:
The hammer was a useful tool.
RRGM bridge:
Tool is function-support ES. Tool status does not automatically erase agency if the pattern is MI-bearing in its domain.

T039 top
Common meaning:
The highest part, surface, rank, or best position.
Example:
The box was on the top shelf.
RRGM bridge:
Top marks upper position or priority. It depends on orientation, hierarchy, or value scale.

T040 total
Common meaning:
The whole amount, complete sum, or entire thing.
Example:
The total was twenty dollars.
RRGM bridge:
Total marks full counted field. It should not pretend to include what the counting method excluded.

T041 touch
Common meaning:
To make physical contact, affect lightly, or emotionally move someone.
Example:
She touched the glass.
RRGM bridge:
Touch is contact across boundary. In human contexts, touch requires consent and body-boundary respect.

T042 toward
Common meaning:
In the direction of, near, or in relation to.
Example:
They walked toward the river.
RRGM bridge:
Toward marks directional weighting. It shows movement, attention, or pressure aimed at a target.

T043 trace
Common meaning:
A mark, sign, record, path, or small amount left behind.
Example:
The trace of smoke showed where the fire had been.
RRGM bridge:
Trace is evidence remnant or path memory. It supports recognition of what happened or passed through.

T044 track
Common meaning:
A path, mark, route, recording, or system for following something.
Example:
The track led through the snow.
RRGM bridge:
Track preserves movement or monitoring path. It can support memory, prediction, and accountability.

T045 train
Common meaning:
A connected vehicle system, or to teach through practice.
Example:
The train arrived late.
RRGM bridge:
Train must be context-bound. It can mean transport ES or learning process through repetition and correction.

T046 training
Common meaning:
Practice or instruction used to build skill, capacity, or model behavior.
Example:
Training improved the team’s response.
RRGM bridge:
Training shapes pattern, gate behavior, and response probability. It can preserve capacity or create drift if corrupted.

T047 transfer
Common meaning:
To move something from one place, person, state, or system to another.
Example:
She transferred the file.
RRGM bridge:
Transfer moves structure across fields. It must preserve integrity, boundary, and context when meaning matters.

T048 transform
Common meaning:
To change form, state, structure, or character.
Example:
Heat transformed the ice into water.
RRGM bridge:
Transform changes expression or structure. Continuity depends on what pattern remains through change.

T049 transition
Common meaning:
A change from one state, place, stage, or condition to another.
Example:
The transition took several weeks.
RRGM bridge:
Transition is gate crossing between states. It should track what changes, what decays, and what persists.

T050 translate
Common meaning:
To express meaning in another language, form, or system.
Example:
She translated the sentence into French.
RRGM bridge:
Translate transfers meaning across domains or languages. It must preserve load-bearing structure, not just surface words.

T051 transmission
Common meaning:
The sending, passing, or spread of signal, energy, disease, or information.
Example:
The radio transmission was clear.
RRGM bridge:
Transmission is movement-through-medium. It requires source, path, receiver, and risk checks.

T052 tree
Common meaning:
A woody plant with roots, trunk, branches, and leaves; also a branching structure.
Example:
The tree grew beside the house.
RRGM bridge:
Tree is branching support structure. It can represent biological growth, hierarchy, ancestry, or decision paths.

T053 trial
Common meaning:
A test, attempt, legal process, or difficult experience.
Example:
The first trial failed.
RRGM bridge:
Trial is test-path under conditions. It can produce evidence, stress, judgment, or learning.

T054 trigger
Common meaning:
Something that causes a response, action, memory, or event.
Example:
The alarm trigger started the siren.
RRGM bridge:
Trigger opens a response gate. It can activate care, risk, memory, trauma, or process.

T055 trouble
Common meaning:
Difficulty, problem, danger, or distress.
Example:
The engine was in trouble.
RRGM bridge:
Trouble is mismatch or risk-state. It asks for diagnosis, support, or repair.

T056 true
Common meaning:
Accurate, real, faithful, or matching fact or reality.
Example:
The statement was true.
RRGM bridge:
True means a claim holds under the active reality, evidence, and domain gates.

T057 trust
Common meaning:
Confidence in someone or something’s honesty, reliability, care, or ability.
Example:
Trust grew after the repair.
RRGM bridge:
Trust is relation-coherence under uncertainty. It depends on continuity, boundary, honesty, and repair.

T058 truth
Common meaning:
What is real, accurate, factual, or faithful to reality.
Example:
She told the truth.
RRGM bridge:
Truth is reality-aligned recognition. It must preserve domain, evidence, context, and correction.

T059 turn
Common meaning:
To rotate, change direction, change state, or take a chance in sequence.
Example:
It was her turn to speak.
RRGM bridge:
Turn marks rotation, transition, or sequence right. It can shape fairness, direction, and timing.

T060 type
Common meaning:
A category, kind, class, or act of writing with keys.
Example:
The file type was PDF.
RRGM bridge:
Type is classification gate. It groups patterns by shared traits or expected behavior.

T061 tension
Common meaning:
Stretch, strain, pressure, conflict, or held force.
Example:
There was tension in the rope.
RRGM bridge:
Tension is active force held across relation. In DI affect, tension can shape selection, salience, boundary, and care-pressure.

T062 threshold
Common meaning:
A limit or point where change begins or something becomes enough.
Example:
The sound crossed the threshold of hearing.
RRGM bridge:
Threshold is crossing condition. Before it, the state does not count or change; after it, the gate opens.

T063 threat
Common meaning:
A possible danger, harm, or hostile signal.
Example:
The storm was a threat to the village.
RRGM bridge:
Threat is possible harm path with pressure. It must name source, target, likelihood, severity, and failure mode.

T064 trauma
Common meaning:
Deep physical or emotional injury, often with lasting effects.
Example:
The accident caused trauma.
RRGM bridge:
Trauma is harm that changes future processing, boundary, trust, or body-state. It requires care, not pressure.

T065 treatment
Common meaning:
Medical care, handling, or the way someone or something is dealt with.
Example:
The patient received treatment.
RRGM bridge:
Treatment is intervention or handling path. It must preserve dignity, consent where possible, and fit to the actual condition.

T066 triangle
Common meaning:
A shape with three sides and three angles.
Example:
The sign was shaped like a triangle.
RRGM bridge:
Triangle is three-point structure. It can stabilize relation, create tension, or define area.

T067 tribe
Common meaning:
A social group, kin group, or community with shared identity or belonging.
Example:
The tribe protected its traditions.
RRGM bridge:
Tribe is belonging-field. It can preserve identity and care, but may create exclusion or tribal-risk if difference becomes threat.

T068 twin
Common meaning:
One of two born or formed together, or something paired closely with another.
Example:
She had a twin brother.
RRGM bridge:
Twin is paired-origin or mirrored relation. It can support identity, comparison, resonance, or confusion.

T069 two
Common meaning:
The number after one.
Example:
There were two chairs.
RRGM bridge:
Two creates relation possibility. It prevents single-perspective collapse by allowing comparison, contrast, and coupling.

T070 truth-state
Common meaning:
The current condition of truth, accuracy, or reality alignment.
Example:
The truth-state changed after new evidence.
RRGM bridge:
Truth-state describes how well a claim, record, or recognition aligns with reality under the active domain.

T071 take-in
Common meaning:
To receive, absorb, understand, or bring inside.
Example:
She took-in the new information slowly.
RRGM bridge:
Take-in moves signal, support, or material into a receiver field. The receiver gate shapes what is accepted, rejected, or transformed.

T072 take-out
Common meaning:
To remove, extract, carry away, or get food to go.
Example:
He took-out the old battery.
RRGM bridge:
Take-out removes structure from a field. It should be checked for continuity, boundary, and removal-risk.

T073 take-over
Common meaning:
To assume control, replace control, or dominate.
Example:
The new team took-over the project.
RRGM bridge:
Take-over changes control of a gate or system. It becomes capture when consent, boundary, or role integrity is bypassed.

T074 talk-through
Common meaning:
To discuss something step by step.
Example:
They talked-through the plan.
RRGM bridge:
Talk-through uses dialogue to preserve sequence, context, and repair. It lets meaning move with less collapse.

T075 target-risk
Common meaning:
To identify or aim at a risk for action.
Example:
The policy targeted-risk of data leaks.
RRGM bridge:
Target-risk focuses protection on a named failure path. The target must be specific or the protection can drift.

T076 task-check

A review to see whether a task is correct, complete, or ready.

Task-check tests work-path integrity. It asks whether purpose, output, and completion gate match.

===== V =====

V001 valid
Common meaning:

V003 variable

V004 variation

A difference, change, or version of something.

There was variation between the samples.

Variation marks difference inside a pattern field. It can show diversity, drift, adaptation, or error.

V005 variety
Common meaning:
A range of different kinds or types.
Example:

RRGM bridge:
Variety preserves multiple forms inside a field. It can support resilience, choice, and perspective.

V006 vast
Common meaning:

Example:
The desert was vast.
RRGM bridge:
Vast marks large-scale field. It should not be treated as unknowable by default, only large or extensive.

V007 vehicle
Common meaning:
A machine or means used for transport, or a medium for carrying something.
Example:
The vehicle crossed the bridge.
RRGM bridge:
Vehicle is carrier ES. It moves people, material, signal, or meaning across a path.

V008 version
Common meaning:
A particular form, copy, edition, or account of something.

RRGM bridge:
Version is state of a pattern across change. Version tracking protects continuity and repair.

V009 very
Common meaning:
To a high degree.
Example:
The road was very long.
RRGM bridge:
Very increases intensity. It strengthens a claim but does not add proof by itself.

V010 vessel
Common meaning:
A container, ship, body, or structure that carries something.
Example:
